# Kensium HRMS — Complete Feature Documentation

_Auto-generated from a live authenticated crawl of **https://ithrms.kensium.com/** on 2026-06-26T21:31:19 (KensiumHR v6)._
_Covers **305 pages**: 7 top menus, their sub-menus and sub-sub-menus, and every Configuration screen._

## How to read this document

Every screen is documented as a **breadcrumb** — `Top Menu > Sub-item > Sub-sub-item` — followed by the controls detected on it:

- **Tabs** — in-page tab strip
- **List view columns** — columns of the page's data grid
- **Actions / buttons** — buttons & action links (Save, Add new, Search, Export, …)
- **Form fields / inputs** — labelled inputs on the page
- **Configuration questions** — yes/no & policy toggles (mostly on Configuration screens)
- **Sections / panels** — headings dividing the page
- **📄 Full page text** — a collapsible block with the complete visible text copied from the page (grids, labels, values, instructions), nav/header/footer chrome removed

Configuration items are grouped by **module** (Exit, Time Off / Leave, Attendance Tracking, …), derived from each screen's URL. Pages marked _(no detail captured)_ are dashboards, redirects, or widget-only screens.

#### Configuration > HRMS > Recruitment > Vacancy Assignment Method

`/Configuration/Configuration/RRAssignmentMethod?parameter=33&SiteId=1`

- **Actions / buttons:** Save · Save & Next · Cancel
- **Form fields / inputs:** Manual · Round robin · Workload

<details><summary>📄 Full page text</summary>

```text
; ;
Vacancy Assignment Method
Setup
|
Pre-Interview Questionnaire

Manual

The user who has been assigned with a role to assign recruiters, shall manually assign the vacancies to respective recruiters.

Round robin

Based on the functional locations assigned to the recruiters, system will automatically assign created vacancies one after the other in a sequence irrespective of the vacancy position created.

Workload

In this method, system shall automatically assign the vacancies to the recruiters considering the number of available vacancies that each recruiter has been assigned with.
```

</details>

### ▸ Surveys

#### Configuration > HRMS > Surveys > Setup

- **Actions / buttons:** Save · Save & Next
- **Form fields / inputs:** Do you want to enable the Survey Module? · Yes · No

<details><summary>📄 Full page text</summary>

```text
; ;
Setup
Survey List

Also allowed for stamp duty, registration fees, and other expenses for purpose of transfer of such property to the assesse. However, if the property is transferred before the expiry of 5 years from the end of the financial year in which possession of such property is obtained by him, the aggregate amount of deduction of income so allowed for various years shall be liable to tax in that year. Contribution towards 15-year Public Provident Fund	Section 80C, 80CCC, 80CCD, 80CCE	 	Under the PPF scheme, Rs 1,50,000 is allowed to be invested in one financial year. The minimum investment required is Rs 500. Interest earned on the PPF account is tax-free. The PPF account matures after 15 years. Receipts on Maturity or withdrawals are tax-free. Money is allowed to be withdrawn after 5 years. Contribution to PPF for an individual can be in the name of the assesse, the spouse, or any child. For a HUF, it can be in the name of any member of the family	Edit

In case the annuity is surrendered before the date of its maturity, the surrender value is taxable in the year of receipt.	Edit

The loan should be taken for the sole purpose of higher education. It could either be for the individual, spouse or children,	Edit
